\def\resethooks{%
  \global\let\SaveRestoreHook\empty
  \global\let\ColumnHook\empty}
\newcommand*{\savecolumns}[1][default]%
  {\g@addto@macro\SaveRestoreHook{\savecolumns[#1]}}
\newcommand*{\restorecolumns}[1][default]%
  {\g@addto@macro\SaveRestoreHook{\restorecolumns[#1]}}
\newcommand*{\aligncolumn}[2]%
  {\g@addto@macro\ColumnHook{\column{#1}{#2}}}

\resethooks

\newcommand{\onelinecommentchars}{\quad-{}- }
\newcommand{\commentbeginchars}{\enskip\{-}
\newcommand{\commentendchars}{-\}\enskip}

\newcommand{\visiblecomments}{%
  \let\onelinecomment=\onelinecommentchars
  \let\commentbegin=\commentbeginchars
  \let\commentend=\commentendchars}

\newcommand{\invisiblecomments}{%
  \let\onelinecomment=\empty
  \let\commentbegin=\empty
  \let\commentend=\empty}

\visiblecomments

\newlength{\blanklineskip}
\setlength{\blanklineskip}{0.66084ex}

\newcommand{\hsindent}[1]{\quad}% default is fixed indentation
\let\hspre\empty
\let\hspost\empty

%% acronyms



\rulerCmdDef{rules4.ANN.fit.scheme}{%
\ensuremath{\ensuremath{o\vdash } ^{ \ensuremath{\leq } } \ensuremath{\sigma } _{ \ensuremath{\Varid{l}} } \ensuremath{\leq \sigma } _{ \ensuremath{\Varid{r}} } \ensuremath{\mathbin{:}\sigma \leadsto \mathcal{C}} }
}
\rulerCmdDef{rules4.ANN.fit.fit}{%
\rulerRule{fit}{ANN}
{%
\ensuremath{o\vdash } ^{ \ensuremath{\cong } } \ensuremath{\sigma } _{ \ensuremath{\Varid{l}} } \ensuremath{\cong \sigma } _{ \ensuremath{\Varid{r}} } \ensuremath{\mathbin{:}\sigma \leadsto \mathcal{C}} 
}
{%
\ensuremath{o\vdash } ^{ \ensuremath{\leq } } \ensuremath{\sigma } _{ \ensuremath{\Varid{l}} } \ensuremath{\leq \sigma } _{ \ensuremath{\Varid{r}} } \ensuremath{\mathbin{:}\sigma \leadsto \mathcal{C}} 
}
}

\rulerCmdDef{rules4.ANN.match.all.scheme}{%
\ensuremath{\ensuremath{o\vdash } ^{ \ensuremath{\cong } } \ensuremath{\sigma } _{ \ensuremath{\Varid{l}} } \ensuremath{\cong \sigma } _{ \ensuremath{\Varid{r}} } \ensuremath{\mathbin{:}\sigma \leadsto \mathcal{C}} }
}
\rulerCmdDef{rules4.ANN.match.all.m.any.l}{%
\rulerRule{m.any.l}{ANN}
{%
}
{%
\ensuremath{o\vdash } ^{ \ensuremath{\cong } } \ensuremath{{\Box}\cong \sigma \mathbin{:}\sigma \leadsto [\mskip1.5mu\allowforspacecorrection \mskip1.5mu]} 
}
}

\rulerCmdDef{rules4.ANN.match.all.m.any.r}{%
\rulerRule{m.any.r}{ANN}
{%
}
{%
\ensuremath{o\vdash } ^{ \ensuremath{\cong } } \ensuremath{\sigma \cong {\Box}\mathbin{:}\sigma \leadsto [\mskip1.5mu\allowforspacecorrection \mskip1.5mu]} 
}
}

\rulerCmdDef{rules4.ANN.match.all.m.con}{%
\rulerRule{m.con}{ANN}
{%
\ensuremath{I} _{ \ensuremath{\mathrm{1}} } \ensuremath{\equiv I} _{ \ensuremath{\mathrm{2}} } \ensuremath{} 
}
{%
\ensuremath{o\vdash } ^{ \ensuremath{\cong } } \ensuremath{I} _{ \ensuremath{\mathrm{1}} } \ensuremath{\cong I} _{ \ensuremath{\mathrm{2}} } \ensuremath{\mathbin{:}I} _{ \ensuremath{\mathrm{2}} } \ensuremath{\leadsto [\mskip1.5mu\allowforspacecorrection \mskip1.5mu]} 
}
}

\rulerCmdDef{rules4.ANN.match.all.m.var}{%
\rulerRule{m.var}{ANN}
{%
\ensuremath{{\nu}} _{ \ensuremath{\mathrm{1}} } \ensuremath{\equiv {\nu}} _{ \ensuremath{\mathrm{2}} } \ensuremath{} 
}
{%
\ensuremath{o\vdash } ^{ \ensuremath{\cong } } \ensuremath{{\nu}} _{ \ensuremath{\mathrm{1}} } \ensuremath{\cong {\nu}} _{ \ensuremath{\mathrm{2}} } \ensuremath{\mathbin{:}{\nu}} _{ \ensuremath{\mathrm{2}} } \ensuremath{\leadsto [\mskip1.5mu\allowforspacecorrection \mskip1.5mu]} 
}
}

\rulerCmdDef{rules4.ANN.match.all.m.var.l1}{%
\rulerRule{m.var.l1}{ANN}
{%
\ensuremath{\textit{fi}_{l-bind}^{+}\in o} 
\\

{%

}

{%

\ensuremath{o\vdash } ^{ \ensuremath{\cong } } \ensuremath{\sigma } _{ \ensuremath{\mathrm{1}} }^{ \ensuremath{\Varid{l}} } \ensuremath{\cong \sigma } _{ \ensuremath{\mathrm{2}} }^{ \ensuremath{\Varid{l}} } \ensuremath{\mathbin{:}\sigma } _{ \ensuremath{\Varid{l}} } \ensuremath{\leadsto \mathcal{C}} _{ \ensuremath{\Varid{l}} } \ensuremath{;{\delta}} 
\\
\ensuremath{o\vdash } ^{ \ensuremath{\cong } } \ensuremath{\mathcal{C}} _{ \ensuremath{\Varid{l}} } \ensuremath{\sigma } _{ \ensuremath{\mathrm{1}} }^{ \ensuremath{\Varid{r}} } \ensuremath{\cong \mathcal{C}} _{ \ensuremath{\Varid{l}} } \ensuremath{\sigma } _{ \ensuremath{\mathrm{2}} }^{ \ensuremath{\Varid{r}} } \ensuremath{\mathbin{:}\sigma } _{ \ensuremath{\Varid{r}} } \ensuremath{\leadsto \mathcal{C}} _{ \ensuremath{\Varid{r}} } \ensuremath{;{\delta}} 
}
{%
\ensuremath{o\vdash } ^{ \ensuremath{\cong } } \ensuremath{(\allowforspacecorrection \sigma } _{ \ensuremath{\mathrm{1}} }^{ \ensuremath{\Varid{l}} } \ensuremath{,\sigma } _{ \ensuremath{\mathrm{1}} }^{ \ensuremath{\Varid{r}} } \ensuremath{)\cong (\allowforspacecorrection \sigma } _{ \ensuremath{\mathrm{2}} }^{ \ensuremath{\Varid{l}} } \ensuremath{,\sigma } _{ \ensuremath{\mathrm{2}} }^{ \ensuremath{\Varid{r}} } \ensuremath{)\mathbin{:}(\allowforspacecorrection \mathcal{C}} _{ \ensuremath{\Varid{r}} } \ensuremath{\sigma } _{ \ensuremath{\Varid{l}} } \ensuremath{,\sigma } _{ \ensuremath{\Varid{r}} } \ensuremath{)\leadsto \mathcal{C}} _{ \ensuremath{\Varid{r}} } \ensuremath{\mathcal{C}} _{ \ensuremath{\Varid{l}} } \ensuremath{;{\delta}} 
}
}

{%

}

\ensuremath{o\vdash } ^{ \ensuremath{\leq } } \ensuremath{\sigma } _{ \ensuremath{\mathrm{1}} } \ensuremath{\leq {\forall} } \overline{ \ensuremath{\alpha } } \ensuremath{.\sigma } _{ \ensuremath{\mathrm{2}} } \ensuremath{\mathbin{:}\sigma \leadsto \mathcal{C};{\delta}} 
}
}

\rulerCmdDef{rules4.TS.match.all.m.exists.l}{%
\rulerRule{m.exists.l}{TS}
{%
\ensuremath{\sigma } _{ \ensuremath{\Varid{i}} } \ensuremath{\equiv \mathcal{C}} _{ \ensuremath{\alpha } } \ensuremath{\sigma } _{ \ensuremath{\mathrm{1}} } \ensuremath{,\;\mathcal{C}} _{ \ensuremath{\alpha } } \ensuremath{\equiv } \overline{ \ensuremath{\alpha \mapsto \Varid{c}} } \ensuremath{,\;} \overline{ \ensuremath{\Varid{c}} } \ensuremath{} \;\mbox{fresh} \ensuremath{} 
\\
\ensuremath{o\vdash } ^{ \ensuremath{\leq } } \ensuremath{\sigma } _{ \ensuremath{\Varid{i}} } \ensuremath{\leq \sigma } _{ \ensuremath{\mathrm{2}} } \ensuremath{\mathbin{:}\sigma \leadsto \mathcal{C};{\delta}} 
}
{%
\ensuremath{o\vdash } ^{ \ensuremath{\leq } } \ensuremath{{\exists} } \overline{ \ensuremath{\alpha } } \ensuremath{.\sigma } _{ \ensuremath{\mathrm{1}} } \ensuremath{\leq \sigma } _{ \ensuremath{\mathrm{2}} } \ensuremath{\mathbin{:}\sigma \leadsto \mathcal{C};{\delta}} 
}
}

\rulerCmdDef{rules4.TS.match.all.m.exists.r}{%
\rulerRule{m.exists.r}{TS}
{%
\ensuremath{\textit{fi}_{r-inst}^{-}\in o} 
\\
\ensuremath{\sigma } _{ \ensuremath{\Varid{i}} } \ensuremath{\equiv \mathcal{C}} _{ \ensuremath{\alpha } } \ensuremath{\sigma } _{ \ensuremath{\mathrm{2}} } \ensuremath{,\;\mathcal{C}} _{ \ensuremath{\alpha } } \ensuremath{\equiv } \overline{ \ensuremath{\alpha \mapsto \Varid{v}} } \ensuremath{,\;} \overline{ \ensuremath{\Varid{v}} } \ensuremath{} \;\mbox{fresh} \ensuremath{} 
\\
\ensuremath{o\vdash } ^{ \ensuremath{\leq } } \ensuremath{\sigma } _{ \ensuremath{\mathrm{1}} } \ensuremath{\leq \sigma } _{ \ensuremath{\Varid{i}} } \ensuremath{\mathbin{:}\sigma \leadsto \mathcal{C}} _{ \ensuremath{\Varid{f}} } \ensuremath{;{\delta}} 
\\
\ensuremath{\mathcal{C}\equiv \mathcal{C}} _{ \ensuremath{\Varid{f}} } \ensuremath{{\backslash}} _{ \ensuremath{} \overline{ \ensuremath{\Varid{v}} } \ensuremath{} }^{ \ensuremath{\Varid{dom}} } \ensuremath{} 
}
{%
\ensuremath{o\vdash } ^{ \ensuremath{\leq } } \ensuremath{\sigma } _{ \ensuremath{\mathrm{1}} } \ensuremath{\leq {\exists} } \overline{ \ensuremath{\alpha } } \ensuremath{.\sigma } _{ \ensuremath{\mathrm{2}} } \ensuremath{\mathbin{:}\mathcal{C}\;(\allowforspacecorrection {\exists} } \overline{ \ensuremath{\alpha } } \ensuremath{.\sigma } _{ \ensuremath{\mathrm{2}} } \ensuremath{)\leadsto \mathcal{C};{\delta}} 
}
}

\rulerCmdDef{rules4.TS.match.all.m.exists.r2}{%
\rulerRule{m.exists.r2}{TS}
{%
\ensuremath{\textit{fi}_{r-inst}^{+}\in o} 
\\
\ensuremath{\sigma } _{ \ensuremath{\Varid{i}} } \ensuremath{\equiv inst} _{ \ensuremath{{\exists}} } \ensuremath{(\allowforspacecorrection {\exists} } \overline{ \ensuremath{\alpha } } \ensuremath{.\sigma } _{ \ensuremath{\mathrm{2}} } \ensuremath{)} 
\\
\ensuremath{o\vdash } ^{ \ensuremath{\leq } } \ensuremath{\sigma } _{ \ensuremath{\mathrm{1}} } \ensuremath{\leq \sigma } _{ \ensuremath{\Varid{i}} } \ensuremath{\mathbin{:}\sigma \leadsto \mathcal{C};{\delta}} 
}
{%
\ensuremath{o\vdash } ^{ \ensuremath{\leq } } \ensuremath{\sigma } _{ \ensuremath{\mathrm{1}} } \ensuremath{\leq {\exists} } \overline{ \ensuremath{\alpha } } \ensuremath{.\sigma } _{ \ensuremath{\mathrm{2}} } \ensuremath{\mathbin{:}\sigma \leadsto \mathcal{C};{\delta}} 
}
}

\rulerCmdDef{rules4.TS.match.all.m.arrow}{%
\rulerRule{m.arrow}{TS}
{%
\ensuremath{\textit{fi}_{r-inst}^{-},\textit{fi}_{r-bind}^{+},\textit{fi}_{l-bind}^{+},o\vdash } ^{ \ensuremath{\cong } } \ensuremath{\sigma } _{ \ensuremath{\mathrm{2}} }^{ \ensuremath{\Varid{a}} } \ensuremath{\cong \sigma } _{ \ensuremath{\mathrm{1}} }^{ \ensuremath{\Varid{a}} } \ensuremath{\mathbin{:}\sigma } _{ \ensuremath{\Varid{a}} } \ensuremath{\leadsto \mathcal{C}} _{ \ensuremath{\Varid{a}} } \ensuremath{;{\delta}} 
\\
\ensuremath{o\vdash } ^{ \ensuremath{\cong } } \ensuremath{\mathcal{C}} _{ \ensuremath{\Varid{a}} } \ensuremath{\sigma } _{ \ensuremath{\mathrm{1}} }^{ \ensuremath{\Varid{r}} } \ensuremath{\cong \mathcal{C}} _{ \ensuremath{\Varid{a}} } \ensuremath{\sigma } _{ \ensuremath{\mathrm{2}} }^{ \ensuremath{\Varid{r}} } \ensuremath{\mathbin{:}\sigma } _{ \ensuremath{\Varid{r}} } \ensuremath{\leadsto \mathcal{C}} _{ \ensuremath{\Varid{r}} } \ensuremath{;{\delta}} 
}
{%
\ensuremath{o\vdash } ^{ \ensuremath{\cong } } \ensuremath{\sigma } _{ \ensuremath{\mathrm{1}} }^{ \ensuremath{\Varid{a}} } \ensuremath{\to \sigma } _{ \ensuremath{\mathrm{1}} }^{ \ensuremath{\Varid{r}} } \ensuremath{\cong \sigma } _{ \ensuremath{\mathrm{2}} }^{ \ensuremath{\Varid{a}} } \ensuremath{\to \sigma } _{ \ensuremath{\mathrm{2}} }^{ \ensuremath{\Varid{r}} } \ensuremath{\mathbin{:}\mathcal{C}} _{ \ensuremath{\Varid{r}} } \ensuremath{\sigma } _{ \ensuremath{\Varid{a}} } \ensuremath{\to \sigma } _{ \ensuremath{\Varid{r}} } \ensuremath{\leadsto \mathcal{C}} _{ \ensuremath{\Varid{r}} } \ensuremath{\mathcal{C}} _{ \ensuremath{\Varid{a}} } \ensuremath{;{\delta}} 
}
}

\rulerCmdDef{rules4.TS.match.all.m.prod}{%
\rulerRule{m.prod}{TS}
{%
\ensuremath{o\vdash } ^{ \ensuremath{\cong } } \ensuremath{\sigma } _{ \ensuremath{\mathrm{1}} }^{ \ensuremath{\Varid{l}} } \ensuremath{\cong \sigma } _{ \ensuremath{\mathrm{2}} }^{ \ensuremath{\Varid{l}} } \ensuremath{\mathbin{:}\sigma } _{ \ensuremath{\Varid{l}} } \ensuremath{\leadsto \mathcal{C}} _{ \ensuremath{\Varid{l}} } \ensuremath{;{\delta}} 
\\
\ensuremath{o\vdash } ^{ \ensuremath{\cong } } \ensuremath{\mathcal{C}} _{ \ensuremath{\Varid{l}} } \ensuremath{\sigma } _{ \ensuremath{\mathrm{1}} }^{ \ensuremath{\Varid{r}} } \ensuremath{\cong \mathcal{C}} _{ \ensuremath{\Varid{l}} } \ensuremath{\sigma } _{ \ensuremath{\mathrm{2}} }^{ \ensuremath{\Varid{r}} } \ensuremath{\mathbin{:}\sigma } _{ \ensuremath{\Varid{r}} } \ensuremath{\leadsto \mathcal{C}} _{ \ensuremath{\Varid{r}} } \ensuremath{;{\delta}} 
}
{%
\ensuremath{o\vdash } ^{ \ensuremath{\cong } } \ensuremath{(\allowforspacecorrection \sigma } _{ \ensuremath{\mathrm{1}} }^{ \ensuremath{\Varid{l}} } \ensuremath{,\sigma } _{ \ensuremath{\mathrm{1}} }^{ \ensuremath{\Varid{r}} } \ensuremath{)\cong (\allowforspacecorrection \sigma } _{ \ensuremath{\mathrm{2}} }^{ \ensuremath{\Varid{l}} } \ensuremath{,\sigma } _{ \ensuremath{\mathrm{2}} }^{ \ensuremath{\Varid{r}} } \ensuremath{)\mathbin{:}(\allowforspacecorrection \mathcal{C}} _{ \ensuremath{\Varid{r}} } \ensuremath{\sigma } _{ \ensuremath{\Varid{l}} } \ensuremath{,\sigma } _{ \ensuremath{\Varid{r}} } \ensuremath{)\leadsto \mathcal{C}} _{ \ensuremath{\Varid{r}} } \ensuremath{\mathcal{C}} _{ \ensuremath{\Varid{l}} } \ensuremath{;{\delta}} 
}
}
